					</p>
					<p class="review-text-full hidden">
						I work as an early childhood educator and always purchase Brown Bear books as gifts for parents in our program to read to their children. This book has a wonderful cadence and rythmn that can be tapped on the board book when read to the child. This is a great way to keep the childs attention while reading the book. It is also exciting when you see the child pick up the book and start tapping and &quot;reading&quot; (as best they can) the book. It also teachers children primary colors and is easily memorized for retelling. I recommend it to everyone with young children - and for gifts.
						<a class="seeless" href="#">see less</a>

			<div class="user-review-heading">Great book! Great price?</div>
			
				<div class="review-text">
					<p class="review-text-half">
						
						I loved reading his book! ... 
						<a class="seemore" href="#">see more</a>
					</p>
					<p class="review-text-full hidden">
						I loved reading his book! I'm not the kind of person who keeps their book copies so they can read them over again, so I was hoping to get this book at the library. Since the library didn't have it, I got a copy from Target. The paperback copy of this book is nice if you don't mind small scratches on the title page. I loved the bok, but I didn't want to pay nine dollars for it when I could borrow it for free from a library.
						<a class="seeless" href="#">see less</a>
					</p>
				</div>
